             <p>
              We will find intelligent extraterrestrial life within 25 years, claims leading alien hunter. He believes mankind will have developed the capability to send electromagnetic signals out into the cosmos
We will find intelligent life on other planets within 25 years, the man behind one of the world\'s most advanced searches for alien life has predicted. Seth Shostak of the SETI (Search for Extraterrestrial Intelligence) Institute made the claim at a Nasa conference looking at advanced technologies.
He believes the key is to keep scanning the skies looking for alien-produced electromagnetic signals.

\'I think we\'ll find E.T. within two dozen years using these sorts of experiments\"\' Shostak said at the 2014 NASA Innovative Advanced Concepts (NIAC) symposium at Stanford University.

              <h3 class="video-title">
               SETI and The Pursuit of Extra-Terrestrial Intelligence w/ Seth Shostak
              </h3>
              <div class="datestamp">
               <span data-trans="Published">
                <span data-trans="published:">
                 published:

               27 Mar 2015
              </div>

            <div class="video-fulltitle" style="display: none;">
             SETI and The Pursuit of Extra-Terrestrial Intelligence w/ Seth Shostak
            </div>
            <div class="video-fulldescription">
             <h3>
              SETI and The Pursuit of Extra-Terrestrial Intelligence w/ Seth Shostak
             </h3>
             <ul class="font_color">
              <li>
               <span data-trans="published:">
                published:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                27 Mar 2015
               </span>
              </li>
              <li>
               <span data-trans="views:">
                views:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                11
               </span>
              </li>
             </ul>
             <p>
              Seth Shostak is the Senior Astronomer at the SETI Institute in Mountain View, California. Inspired by a book about the solar system he read at the age of ten, he began his career with a degree in physics from Princeton University and a PhD in astronomy from the California Institute of Technology before working with radio telescopes in the US and the Netherlands to uncover how the universe will end. In 1999, he produced twelve 30-minute lectures on audio-tape and video titled \"The Search for Intelligent Life in Space\" for the Teaching Company and has hosted SETIs Big Picture Science podcast since 2002. In 2010, he was elected as a Fellow of the Committee for Skeptical Inquiry and is the Chair of the International Academy of Astronautics SETI Permanent Study Group. He has published four books, nearly 300 popular articles on astronomy, technology, film and television and gives frequent talks to both young and adult audiences.

In this interview:

Dr. Shostak answers a question from GLP\'s Dr. Astro! 6:50
What is the first-contact protocol? 12:24
How rare is humanoid life? 24:03
Is Seth Shostak a government shill? 30:44...
             </p>
            </div>

              <h3 class="video-title">
               Extraterrestrial Multiverse Civilizations
              </h3>
              <div class="datestamp">

             Extraterrestrial Multiverse Civilizations
            </div>
            <div class="video-fulldescription">
             <h3>
              Extraterrestrial Multiverse Civilizations
             </h3>
             <ul class="font_color">
              <li>
               <span data-trans="published:">
                published:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                23 Mar 2015
               </span>
              </li>
              <li>
               <span data-trans="views:">
                views:

               <span class="strong">

               </span>
              </li>

             <p>
              The Dimensional Ecology of the Omniverse: is a New Book Reveals New Scientific Evidence of the \'Multiverse\' and \'Omniverse\' Concepts.

Written by Yale graduate Alfred Lambremont Webre, this startling book examines the idea that humanity lives on a planet in one universe that exists in a multiverse within an Omniverse.

Webre, a leading thinker in the field, details his arguments with simple and stunning clarity.

In 2000, author Alfred Lambremont Webre released his book, \'Exopolitics: A Decade of Contact\', which founded Exopolitics, the science of relations among intelligent civilizations in the multiverse. Immediately, Webre became a leading extraterrestrial and time-travel whistleblower, attracting great attention from both scientific and political communities.

With \'The Dimensional Ecology of the Omniverse\', Webre cements his role as the developer of the Exopolitics and Dimensional Ecology models of the Omniverse.

As Webre points out, the details of his book are vital to help readers understand the connection between science and spirituality.

\"The book reveals new scientific evidence on matters like the afterlife, the human soul, reincarnation, and God,\" says Webre. \"God used to be a matter of personal belief, but Science is confirming spirituality. As the book also shows, Scientists now know that humanity lives on one planet in one solar system in one universe in a multiverse that has, as one Scientist wrote: \"a humungous\" number of universes in it. The book\'s evidence shows that souls and God in the spiritual dimensions are co-creating the universes of the multivers...
             </p>

              <h3 class="video-title">
               Mars Colonies, Alien Bloodlines &amp; Illuminati in Space with Alfred Webre
              </h3>
              <div class="datestamp">
               <span data-trans="Published">
                <span data-trans="published:">

             Mars Colonies, Alien Bloodlines &amp; Illuminati in Space with Alfred Webre
            </div>
            <div class="video-fulldescription">
             <h3>
              Mars Colonies, Alien Bloodlines &amp; Illuminati in Space with Alfred Webre
             </h3>
             <ul class="font_color">
              <li>
               <span data-trans="published:">
                published:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                21 Mar 2015
               </span>
              </li>
              <li>
               <span data-trans="views:">
                views:
               </span>
               <span class="strong">
                301
               </span>

             <p>
              Mars colonies, extraterrestrial bloodlines and conflicts, and the influence of the Bilderberg Group, Illuminati, and Skull &amp; Bones are all explored with Alfred Webre. How Mars became a dead planet, the possible depopulation of Earth, and our planets true alien elite--from Annunaki to Reptilian Grays--are demystified as we explore the conspiracy to move the elite to a home on Mars. Is the multi-dimensional universe on a changing paradigm away from the zero-sum game of warfare? What did Nikola Tesla know about life on Mars? And what role does Dick Cheney play in the manipulation of mankind? Explore the secrets of the illuminati in space in this uncensored Buzzsaw interview, hosted by Sean Stone.

GUEST BIO:
Alfred Lambremont Webre, JD, MEd - Alfred\'s book, Exopolitics: A Decade of Contact (2000), founded Exopolitics, the science of relations among intelligent civilizations in the multiverse. Using advanced quantum access technology, the U.S. Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency (DARPA) and the Central Intelligence Agency (CIA) time traveled Alfred\'s book, Exopolitics: Politics, Government, and Law in the Universe (2005), from 2005 back to 1971, when an unwitting Alfred was examined by a group of approximately 50 CIA and DARPA officials who knew Alfred would be a leading future extraterrestrial and time-travel whistleblower, and would become the developer of the Exopolitics and Dimensional Ecology models of the Omniverse.

Alfred\'s Bio: 

Alfred is a graduate of Yale University and Yale Law School in international law and was a Fulbright Scholar in international economic integration in Uruguay. He has taught economics at Yale University and constitutional law at the University of Texas. Alfred was general counsel to the New York City Environmental Protection Administration, a futurist at Stanford Research Institute (where he directed the proposed 1977 Carter White House extraterrestrial communication study), and was a NGO delegate to the United Nations and the UNISPACE conference.

 Alfred is active with non-profit organizations concerned with peace, the environment, human rights and social justice, consciousness, and intelligent life in the Omniverse, including the Mars Anomaly Research Society (MARS).

             <p>
              Former National Security Agency (NSA) contractor Edward Snowden revealed documents providing incontrovertible proof that an alien/extraterrestrial intelligence agenda is driving US domestic and international policy, and has been doing so since at least 1945, some media reports said.

A stunning Federal Security Services (FSB) report on the nearly two million highly classified top-secret documents obtained from the United States Department of Defense (DOD) run National Security Agency-Central Security Service (NSA/CSS) by the American ex-patriot Edward Snowden states that this information is providing \"incontrovertible proof\" that an \"alien/extraterrestrial intelligence agenda\" is driving US domestic and international policy, and has been doing so since at least 1945,

            <div class="mediawiki ltr sitedir-ltr ns-0 skin-vector">
             <div class="mwp">
              <img height="80" src="http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/CSICON_2011-Seth_Shostak.JPG/120px-CSICON_2011-Seth_Shostak.JPG" style="float:right; padding: 0 0 10px 10px" width="120"/>
              <p>
               <b>
                Seth Shostak
               </b>
               (born July 20, 1943) is an
               <a href="http://wn.com/United_States" title="United States">
                American
               </a>
               <a href="http://wn.com/Astronomer" title="Astronomer">
                astronomer
               </a>
               . He grew up in
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/Arlington,_VA" title="Arlington, VA">
                Arlington, VA
               </a>
               and earned his
               <a href="http://wn.com/Physics" title="Physics">
                physics
               </a>
               degree from
               <a href="http://wn.com/Princeton_University" title="Princeton University">
                Princeton University
               </a>
               and a
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/Ph.D." title="Ph.D.">
                Ph.D.
               </a>
               in
               <a href="http://wn.com/Astronomy" title="Astronomy">
                astronomy
               </a>
               from the
               <a href="http://wn.com/California_Institute_of_Technology" title="California Institute of Technology">
                California Institute of Technology
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               He is the Senior Astronomer at the
               <a href="http://wn.com/SETI_Institute" title="SETI Institute">
                SETI Institute
               </a>
               in
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/Mountain_View,_Santa_Clara_County,_California" title="Mountain View, Santa Clara County, California">
                Mountain View, California
               </a>
               , and the 2004 winner of the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Klumpke-Roberts_Award" title="Klumpke-Roberts Award">
                Klumpke-Roberts Award
               </a>
               awarded by the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Astronomical_Society_of_the_Pacific" title="Astronomical Society of the Pacific">
                Astronomical Society of the Pacific
               </a>
               in recognition of his outstanding contributions to the public understanding and appreciation of astronomy.
              </p>
              <p>
               Before his involvement with
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/SETI" title="SETI">
                SETI
               </a>
               research, he used
               <a href="http://wn.com/Radio_telescope" title="Radio telescope">
                radio telescopes
               </a>
               in
               <a href="http://wn.com/United_States" title="United States">
                the USA
               </a>
               and the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">
                Netherlands
               </a>
               , searching for clues to the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Ultimate_fate_of_the_universe" title="Ultimate fate of the universe">
                ultimate fate of the universe
               </a>
               by analyzing galaxy motion.
              </p>
              <p>
               In addition to his experience as an active participant in SETI research, Shostak is also involved as a science educator. He presented twelve 30-minute lectures on audio-tape and video titled "The Search for Intelligent Life in Space" for the
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/Teaching_Company" title="Teaching Company">
                Teaching Company
               </a>
               in 1999.
              </p>
              <p>
               Since February 2002 Shostak has hosted the SETI Institute's radio program
               <a href="http://wn.com/Are_We_Alone?" title="Are We Alone?">
                Are We Alone?
               </a>
               which was renamed "Big Picture Science" in July 2011. Each week, Shostak interviews guests about the latest scientific research on a variety of topics:
               <a href="http://wn.com/Cosmology" title="Cosmology">
                cosmology
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Physics" title="Physics">
                physics
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Genetics" title="Genetics">
                genetics
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Paleontology" title="Paleontology">
                paleontology
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://wn.com/Evolutionary_biology" title="Evolutionary biology">
                evolutionary biology
               </a>
               and
               <a href="http://wn.com/Astrobiology" title="Astrobiology">
                astrobiology
               </a>
               .
               <i>
                <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://wn.com/Big_Picture_Science" title="Big Picture Science">
                 Big Picture Science
                </a>
               </i>
               is distributed on the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Public_Radio_Satellite_System" title="Public Radio Satellite System">
                Public Radio Satellite System
               </a>
               and the
               <a href="http://wn.com/Public_Radio_Exchange" title="Public Radio Exchange">
                Public Radio Exchange
               </a>
               and is available for download at the SETI Institute's website and through podcasts.
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>

  <script>
   function defineAspectRatio() {

            jQuery('.image-frame img').each(function(index) {

                jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');

                var parentWidth = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').width();
                var parentHeight = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').height();
                var imgWidth = jQuery(this).width();
                var imgHeight = jQuery(this).height();

                    if(imgWidth == imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('squa');

                        jQuery('#tracker').append('|' + imgWidth + '&amp;' + parentWidth + '|');

                        if(parentHeight &lt; parentWidth) {
                            jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                            jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        } else if(parentHeight &gt; parentWidth) {
                            jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                            jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        }

                    } else if(imgWidth &lt; imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('port');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                    } else if(imgWidth &gt; imgHeight) {
                        jQuery(this).addClass('land');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                    }

                });

imageShimmy();

};

function imageShimmy() {

    jQuery('.image-frame img').each(function(index) {

        var parentWidth_sp = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').width();
        var parentHeight_sp = jQuery(this).parent('.image-frame').height();
        var imgWidth_sp = jQuery(this).width();
        var imgHeight_sp = jQuery(this).height();

        var imgWidthShimmy = (imgWidth_sp - parentWidth_sp)/2;
        var imgHeightShimmy = (imgHeight_sp - parentHeight_sp)/2;

                    if(jQuery(this).hasClass('land') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &lt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('land') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &gt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('port') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &lt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('port') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &gt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &lt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgHeight_sp &gt; parentHeight_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('width', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('height', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-top', '-' + imgHeightShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &lt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    } else if(jQuery(this).hasClass('squa') &amp;&amp; imgWidth_sp &gt; parentWidth_sp) {
                        jQuery(this).css('height', '100%');
                        jQuery(this).css('width', 'auto');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin', '0');
                        jQuery(this).css('margin-left', '-' + imgWidthShimmy + 'px');
                    };

                    jQuery(this).animate({
                        opacity: 1},
                        200, function() {
                        // stuff to do after animation is complete
                    });


                });
}



jQuery(window).load(function() {

    defineAspectRatio();

});
  </script>

    $(function(){
				var playerPosition = $('#playercontainer1').offset();

		        $(".search-type a").click(function () {
		
		            var search_type = $(this).data('type');		
		            $("#search-selector").val(search_type);
		                if(!$(this).hasClass("active"))
		                {
		                    $(".search-type a").removeClass("active");		
		                    $(this).addClass("active");		
		                }
		        });
		        $('#mainsearch').submit(function(event) {
		            var search_type = $("#search-selector").val();					
		            if(search_type == 'videos') {
		                var search_string = $(".top_query").val();
		                search_string = search_string.toLowerCase().replace(/[\.\/\: _!]+/g, '_');
		                window.open('http://wn.com/' + search_string, '_blank');
		                return false; // do not submit the form
		            }else{
		                return true;
		            }
		         });
				 
				$(".gotop").live("click", function(){
					$('html, body').animate({scrollTop: playerPosition.top}, "slow");

  					$(".logo-bm li").removeClass("active");

    function get_ip_data_and_focus(callback) {
        $.getJSON( "http://ip-api.com/json/?callback=", function(data) {
            weather_data = data;
            country_code = geoip_country_code();
			var country_code = data.countryCode;
				var country_code = country_code.toLowerCase();
				var country = data.country;
				var geo_obj = $('.weather-wdgt');
				var city = data.city;
				var user_country = data.country;
				var lat = data.lat;
				var lng = data.lon;
				$('.user-country').html(country);
				if (city.length &gt; 1) {
					$('.user-city').prepend(city).show();
				}
				$('.flag').addClass('flag-'+country_code);
				var sel = $('#country option').filter(function(index) {
						return ($(this).text() == country)
				});
				var countryArray = ["Argentina", "Australia", "Brazil", "Canada", "Colombia", "Egypt", "France", "Germany", "India", "Indonesia", "Italy", "Japan", "Iran", "Mexico", "Morocco", "Nigeria", "Pakistan", "Philippines", "Russia", "Saudi Arabia", "South Africa", "South Korea", "Spain", "Thailand", "Turkey", "United Kingdom", "United States", "Vietnam" ];
				if( $.inArray(country, countryArray) == -1 ){
	    			$('#country').append('&lt;option selected value="'+ country +'"&gt;'+ country +'&lt;/option&gt;');
	 			}else{
				 	$('#country').val(country).attr('selected', 'selected');
				}
				showCountrySelection(data);
				if (city.length &lt; 1) {
					city = user_country;
				}
	            	var table_body = "";
	            	 $.each(data, function(k, v) {
	      				get_weather_data(geo_obj, lat, lng, country_code);

        });

		// look for languages alternatives using our geonaming service
		function showCountrySelection(geocode_data) {
			jQuery.ajax({
                url: '/api/upge/cheetah-photo-search/geoname',
                data: {country: geocode_data.countryCode, style: 'full'},
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                type: 'GET',
                success: function(data, status) {
                    if (data.geonames) {
                        var geonamelangs = data.geonames[0].languages
                        langs = geonamelangs.split(',')
                        if (langs.length == 0) {
                        	return false;
                        }
                        // only pick the first language
                        first_lang = langs[0]
						if (window.available_langs[first_lang] == undefined) {
							$('#language option').filter(function () {
						   return ($(this).text() == 'English');
							}).attr('selected','selected');
						}
						var lang = window.available_langs[first_lang].langname;

						$('#language option').filter(function () {
						   return ($(this).text() == lang);
							}).attr('selected','selected');

                    }
                }
            });
		}



    get_ip_data_and_focus();

    var geoip_city = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.city;
    };
    var geoip_country_name = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.country;
    };
    var geoip_country_code = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.countryCode;
    };
    var geoip_latitude = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.lat;
    };
    var geoip_longitude = function() {
        if (weather_data == undefined) {
            return '';
        }
        return weather_data.lon;
    };
	function get_weather_data(geo_obj, lat, lng, country_code){
		  first_geo_data = true;
		  var global_geo_obj = geo_obj;
		  jQuery.ajax({
		      data: {
		          lat: jQuery.trim(lat),
		          lng: jQuery.trim(lng),
		          cnt: 1,
		      },
		      dataType: 'jsonp',
		      url: 'http://article.wn.com/api/upge/cheetah-photo-search/weather_findcity',
		      success: function(data) {
		          //weather_data = data.list[0];  ;
		          weather_info = ''
		          for (idx in data.list) {
		              weather_data = data.list[idx]
		              if (weather_data) {
		                weather = weather_data.weather[0]
				  		tempC = parseInt(parseFloat(weather_data.main.temp)-273.15)
				 		tempF = parseInt(tempC*1.8+32)
						weather_info += '&lt;img src="http://cdn0.wn.com/or/images/weather/95/'+weather.icon+'.png" alt="" class="pull-left" /&gt;'
						if (country_code == 'us'){
							weather_info += '&lt;p class="pull-left"&gt;'+tempF+'&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="pull-left letter"&gt;F&lt;/span&gt;'
						}else{
							weather_info += '&lt;p class="pull-left"&gt;'+tempC+'&lt;/p&gt;&lt;span class="fa fa-circle-o pull-left"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="pull-left letter"&gt;C&lt;/span&gt;'
						}
		             }
		          }
		          global_geo_obj.html(weather_info);
		      },
		  });
		};
		function loadLocalNews(country) {
			if(! country){
				var country = $("#country").val().toLowerCase();
			};
			var language = $("#language").val().toLowerCase();
            var sub = (language=='english'?'edition/'+country:'local/'+language)
            document.location = 'http://wn.com/#/'+sub;
        }
